<div id="review_158274399" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/158274399" />
    <a title="#ReadAllTheBooks" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4436152-readallthebooks"><img alt="#ReadAllTheBooks" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1288335161p2/4436152.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/158274399?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="#ReadAllTheBooks" class="user" itemprop="url" name="#ReadAllTheBooks" href="/user/show/4436152-readallthebooks">#ReadAllTheBooks</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4436152-readallthebooks?shelf=amazon-vine">amazon-vine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4436152-readallthebooks?shelf=murder">murder</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4436152-readallthebooks?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4436152-readallthebooks?shelf=horror">horror</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4436152-readallthebooks?shelf=male-lead-character">male-lead-character</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4436152-readallthebooks?shelf=creepy">creepy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4436152-readallthebooks?shelf=gothic">gothic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4436152-readallthebooks?shelf=supernatural">supernatural</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer158274399" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1148595641055139051">One thing is absolutely certain about this book: it's not something that will appeal to every reader. If you're looking for a Stephen King or Dean Koontz type of read, you'll probably want to look elsewhere. If you're looking for something along the lines of Shirley Jackson or Michael Koryta, then this is the book for you. <br/><br/>The story starts out at a crawl & I have to admit that it took me a while to really connect with the story. I really didn't get hooked until about 70-80 pages in, so I'll just</span>
  <span id="freeText1148595641055139051" style="display:none">One thing is absolutely certain about this book: it's not something that will appeal to every reader. If you're looking for a Stephen King or Dean Koontz type of read, you'll probably want to look elsewhere. If you're looking for something along the lines of Shirley Jackson or Michael Koryta, then this is the book for you. <br /><br />The story starts out at a crawl &amp; I have to admit that it took me a while to really connect with the story. I really didn't get hooked until about 70-80 pages in, so I'll just caution people to keep with it. Once the story picks up you won't be able to put it down. <br /><br />A lot of emphasis is put upon the atmosphere of the book &amp; the general surroundings, so if you're a fan of world building then you'll love this book. I never had to wonder what anything looked like or what the emotions in the book were supposed to be. Evans does a wonderful job of showing you exactly what's going on. <br /><br />But I do have to repeat that this book isn't for everyone. It's a wonderfully slow gothic tale &amp; it's well done, but it's not the nail biter that I was hoping it would be. Enthralling &amp; hypnotic towards the end, but not exactly scary to be honest. <br /><br />(ARC provided by amazon vine)</span>
  <a data-text-id="1148595641055139051" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_947735780" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/947735780" />
    <a title="Zeke Gonzalez" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31702416-zeke-gonzalez"><img alt="Zeke Gonzalez" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1471326570p2/31702416.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/947735780?book_show_action=true">Nov 14, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zeke Gonzalez" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zeke Gonzalez" href="/user/show/31702416-zeke-gonzalez">Zeke Gonzalez</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780061728280" href="/book/show/11889162-the-white-devil">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer947735780" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6508509007828624381">In The White Devil, Justin Evans weaves together coming-of-age themes, literary history, and a deeply disturbing ghost story with a deft hand and beautifully crafted prose. The novel falls into a niche genre which bridges the gap between gothic horror and the modern world through the lens of literature and poetic history, and The White Devil navigates between the two with delightful aplomb. (See The Demonologist by Andrew Pyper or A Head Full of Ghosts by Paul Tremblay for other exquisite exampl</span>
  <span id="freeText6508509007828624381" style="display:none">In The White Devil, Justin Evans weaves together coming-of-age themes, literary history, and a deeply disturbing ghost story with a deft hand and beautifully crafted prose. The novel falls into a niche genre which bridges the gap between gothic horror and the modern world through the lens of literature and poetic history, and The White Devil navigates between the two with delightful aplomb. (See The Demonologist by Andrew Pyper or A Head Full of Ghosts by Paul Tremblay for other exquisite examples of this hybrid genre). I loved Justin Evans’ quiet attention to detail in the setting &amp; subject matter and the crisp, engaging characters who develop and unfold over the course of the story. Of course, I would already love any book that has these features, but on top of this enthralling storytelling is also an incredibly creepy and unsettling ghost which, in a single shocking and horrifying scene, became one of the scariest ghosts I’ve ever had the pleasure of reading about. Well done. Overall, The White Devil is a fantastically uncanny and propulsive story which showcases Justin Evans’ considerable literary talents.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6508509007828624381" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_257221519" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/257221519" />
    <a title="Ange" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5605084-ange"><img alt="Ange" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1423648233p2/5605084.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/257221519?book_show_action=true">Jan 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ange" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ange" href="/user/show/5605084-ange">Ange</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer257221519" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7162928852603776066">My 15 year old daughter received this as a gift (not from me) and she read it before I did. She kept warning me that I might be shocked by some of the language and content. I told her that I'm not easily shocked. However after reading it I was slightly suprised that it had been given to her. Although the school setting makes it potentially interesting to teenagers, I think it is probably more appropriate for older teenagers (17 -18 plus) - some of the sexual content may make it a bit confronting</span>
  <span id="freeText7162928852603776066" style="display:none">My 15 year old daughter received this as a gift (not from me) and she read it before I did. She kept warning me that I might be shocked by some of the language and content. I told her that I'm not easily shocked. However after reading it I was slightly suprised that it had been given to her. Although the school setting makes it potentially interesting to teenagers, I think it is probably more appropriate for older teenagers (17 -18 plus) - some of the sexual content may make it a bit confronting for younger teenagers. Having said that, I really enjoyed it. Although the device of having an troubled American student sent to an English public school to sort him out seemed a bit obvious, there was a lot of atmosphere, and I think that the well-drawn adult characters added a lot of depth. Mr Hawkes, the housemaster, the woman librarian, and Sir Andrew Vine, really helped to lift this book above the average. I don't know a lot about Byron, but wasn't a disadvantage. Well worth reading.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7162928852603776066" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christine" href="/user/show/1605591-christine">Christine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1605591-christine?shelf=fantasy-urban">fantasy-urban</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1605591-christine?shelf=dnf">dnf</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer664822232" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13809970119333218282">I like slow and gothic. What I don't understand in the logic of this book are the following quibbles-<br/><br/>1. A poet writing a play about Bryon has only a small volume of select poetry? You can find paperback versions of the complete poems.<br/><br/>2. An American boy who went to a very liberal school that celebrates coming out is surprised that people can be bi.<br/><br/>3. The sheer fact that American girls are seen to be very easyand stupid. Not surprising when looking at the viewpoint, but when tied into the fact tha</span>
  <span id="freeText13809970119333218282" style="display:none">I like slow and gothic. What I don't understand in the logic of this book are the following quibbles-<br /><br />1. A poet writing a play about Bryon has only a small volume of select poetry? You can find paperback versions of the complete poems.<br /><br />2. An American boy who went to a very liberal school that celebrates coming out is surprised that people can be bi.<br /><br />3. The sheer fact that American girls are seen to be very easyand stupid. Not surprising when looking at the viewpoint, but when tied into the fact that there is only one likable girl and all the other girls are gossips, it tends to wear thin.<br /><br />However, those are my quibbles. Number 3 is also a a big turn off for me since reading the Anita Blake novels killed my tolerance for it.<br /><br />I will say that Evans does a wonderful job of evoking mood. He's really good at the mood. It was the mood that got me as far as I did (around page 200).</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/175837177" />
    <a title="Caitlin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2209914-caitlin"><img alt="Caitlin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1239417820p2/2209914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/175837177?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Caitlin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Caitlin" href="/user/show/2209914-caitlin">Caitlin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer175837177" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15861022059965635460">I am always on the lookout for a good college/boarding school story. It's all Donna Tartt's fault that I'm usually disappointed - nothing is ever as good as <i>The Secret History</i>.<br/><br/>I gave <i>The White Devil</i> a try, though - boarding school, murder, the ghost of Lord Byron, various kinds of evildoing - works for me. Except it only sort of worked for me. The beginning was good, then it became sort of okay, and then it pretty much just fell apart.<br/><br/>Mr. Evans is a good writer, but this story just didn't connec</span>
  <span id="freeText15861022059965635460" style="display:none">I am always on the lookout for a good college/boarding school story. It's all Donna Tartt's fault that I'm usually disappointed - nothing is ever as good as <i>The Secret History</i>.<br /><br />I gave <i>The White Devil</i> a try, though - boarding school, murder, the ghost of Lord Byron, various kinds of evildoing - works for me. Except it only sort of worked for me. The beginning was good, then it became sort of okay, and then it pretty much just fell apart.<br /><br />Mr. Evans is a good writer, but this story just didn't connect to anything I care about. Maybe I've read one too many books about rich, whiny American kids to be able to handle another.<br /><br />Still - mildly entertaining, but could have used a better main character - Andrew was pretty two-dimensional and I want more than that from a read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15861022059965635460" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kj1M2tCgyMMLyuN7HAeJGL5sXVR0ofB5/7R0vhfvOZ31Wu2Vm9ykKOxOLnSJLn7ZkDnLxnv8ZC2RhMBNlwUeTA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('cWQXe5QpbsnM/CK3VY1gke0eT1FiTFnfWeNl3akik1IWA7Y031UCIit477jApJdQw0vZw20RzYs309EuKci0gw==')})
  }

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_52141547').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_52141547').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_52141547').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>

  <span id="freeText9073095191146427854" style="display:none">Justin Evans is a digital media executive based in New York City where he lives with his family. His first novel, A Good and Happy Child, was named a Best Book of 2007 by the Washington Post, was translated into six languages, and optioned by a major film studio. Justin attended Harrow School for one year at the end of the eighties.<br /><br />Write to Justin at justin@justinevans.com.</span>
